{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_018dsVATxjSHzELgiDGRFqWP","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_011Ce6W6PpqsyUMCfJmL385f","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/README.md","content":"# Non-Legacy Mail Decryption Bug - Regression Test\n\n## Overview\n\nThis directory contains a comprehensive regression test for a critical bug in tutanota where **non-legacy mails fail to decrypt** because owner-encrypted session keys are not propagated when loading related entities.\n\n## The Bug\n\n### Symptoms\nUsers with accounts using the new (non-legacy) permission model report:\n- Opening emails results in blank message bodies\n- Reply-to addresses are missing\n- Attachment listings cannot be loaded\n- Browser console shows \"Missing decryption key\" errors\n- Mail indexer/search fails silently with decryption errors\n\n### Root Cause\n\nWhen loading supplementary mail data (body content, draft details, attachments), the session key needed for decryption is available from the parent mail object but **is not being passed through** to the entity loading and caching layers.\n\nSpecifically:\n1. The `Mail` entity has `_ownerEncSessionKey` (owner-encrypted session key)\n2. Related entities like `MailDetailsBlob`, `File`, etc. also have `_ownerEncSessionKey`\n3. When loading these related entities using `EntityClient.loadMultiple()`, there's **no way to pass the ownerKey**\n4. The decryption system tries to resolve the session key without the ownerKey\n5. It fails because it can't decrypt `_ownerEncSessionKey` without the ownerKey\n6. The loaded entity ends up with `_errors` set, indicating decryption failure\n\n## Test File Location\n\n- **TypeScript Documentation**: `/workspace/regression_test.test.ts`\n- **JavaScript Test**: `/workspace/regression_test.test.js` (Jest-executable version)\n\n## Running the Test\n\n### Using Jest (Recommended)\n\n```bash\n# Run the JavaScript version (no transpiler needed)\nnpx jest --timeout=60000 /workspace/regression_test.test.js\n\n# Or with the shell script\nbash /workspace/run-test.sh\n```\n\n### With TypeScript\n\nTo run the `.test.ts` version with Jest, you need ts-jest:\n\n```bash\nnpm install -g ts-jest\n# Then update jest.config.js to include:\n# preset: 'ts-jest'\n\nnpx jest --timeout=60000 /workspace/regression_test.test.ts\n```\n\n## Code Locations That Need Fixing\n\n### 1. **EntityClient.ts** (Core API)\n- File: `/app/src/api/common/EntityClient.ts`\n- Line: ~77-79\n- Current: `loadMultiple<T>(typeRef, listId, elementIds)`\n- Needed: `loadMultiple<T>(typeRef, listId, elementIds, ownerKey?)`\n\n### 2. **EntityRestClient.ts** (REST Implementation)\n- File: `/app/src/api/worker/rest/EntityRestClient.ts`\n- Location 1 - Line ~173: Add ownerKey parameter to `loadMultiple`\n- Location 2 - Line ~247: Modify `_decryptMapAndMigrate` to accept and use ownerKey\n\n### 3. **MailUtils.ts** (Mail Loading)\n- File: `/app/src/mail/model/MailUtils.ts`\n- Line: ~405\n- Current:\n  ```typescript\n  return entityClient.loadMultiple(MailDetailsBlobTypeRef, listIdPart(mailDetailsId), [elementIdPart(mailDetailsId)])\n  ```\n- Should pass: `mail._ownerEncSessionKey` or derived ownerKey\n\n### 4. **MailIndexer.ts** (Search/Indexing)\n- File: `/app/src/api/worker/search/MailIndexer.ts`\n- Same issue when loading MailDetailsBlob for indexing\n\n### 5. **MailViewerViewModel.ts** (UI Rendering)\n- File: `/app/src/mail/view/MailViewerViewModel.ts`\n- Same issue when loading attachments\n\n### 6. **ConversationViewModel.ts** (Conversation Loading)\n- File: `/app/src/mail/view/ConversationViewModel.ts`\n- Similar issues with batch loading\n\n## Implementation Strategy\n\n### Minimum Fix (Phase 1)\n1. Add `ownerKey?` parameter to `EntityClient.loadMultiple()`\n2. Add `ownerKey?` parameter to `EntityRestClient.loadMultiple()`\n3. Pass ownerKey through to `_decryptMapAndMigrate()`\n4. Modify `_decryptMapAndMigrate()` to use ownerKey when available\n5. Update callers in `MailUtils.loadMailDetails()` to pass ownerKey\n\n### Complex Scenarios (Phase 2)\nFor batch operations where entities have different owner keys:\n- Option A: Load entities one by one when they have different keys\n- Option B: Use a `Map<elementId, ownerKey>` to track per-entity keys\n- Option C: Implement a callback mechanism for per-entity key resolution\n\n## Key Files for Reference\n\n- **Bug Documentation**: `/workspace/regression_test.test.ts`\n- **Configuration**: `/workspace/jest.config.js`\n- **Runner Script**: `/workspace/run-test.sh`\n\n## Test Status\n\n✅ The regression test is self-contained and documents the bug comprehensively.\n❌ The actual bug fix has not been implemented yet.\n\n## Expected Behavior After Fix\n\nOnce the fix is implemented:\n1.
